\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ 5/15/11\ v1.09\ -\/\ Initial\ stable\ release.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ Low-\/level\ Deflate/Inflate\ implementation\ notes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Compression:\ Use\ the\ "{}tdefl"{}\ API's.\ The\ compressor\ supports\ raw,\ static,\ and\ dynamic\ blocks,\ lazy\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ greedy\ parsing,\ match\ length\ filtering,\ RLE-\/only,\ and\ Huffman-\/only\ streams.\ It\ performs\ and\ compresses}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ approximately\ as\ well\ as\ zlib.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Decompression:\ Use\ the\ "{}tinfl"{}\ API's.\ The\ entire\ decompressor\ is\ implemented\ as\ a\ single\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ coroutine:\ see\ tinfl\_decompress().\ It\ supports\ decompression\ into\ a\ 32KB\ (or\ larger\ power\ of\ 2)\ wrapping\ buffer,\ or\ into\ a\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ block\ large\ enough\ to\ hold\ the\ entire\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ The\ low-\/level\ tdefl/tinfl\ API's\ do\ not\ make\ any\ use\ of\ dynamic\ memory\ allocation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ zlib-\/style\ API\ notes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ miniz.c\ implements\ a\ fairly\ large\ subset\ of\ zlib.\ There's\ enough\ functionality\ present\ for\ it\ to\ be\ a\ drop-\/in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ zlib\ replacement\ in\ many\ apps:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ z\_stream\ struct,\ optional\ memory\ allocation\ callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ deflateInit/deflateInit2/deflate/deflateReset/deflateEnd/deflateBound}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ inflateInit/inflateInit2/inflate/inflateEnd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ compress,\ compress2,\ compressBound,\ uncompress}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ CRC-\/32,\ Adler-\/32\ -\/\ Using\ modern,\ minimal\ code\ size,\ CPU\ cache\ friendly\ routines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Supports\ raw\ deflate\ streams\ or\ standard\ zlib\ streams\ with\ adler-\/32\ checking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ The\ callback\ API's\ are\ not\ implemented\ yet.\ No\ support\ for\ gzip\ headers\ or\ zlib\ static\ dictionaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ I've\ tried\ to\ closely\ emulate\ zlib's\ various\ flavors\ of\ stream\ flushing\ and\ return\ status\ codes,\ but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ there\ are\ no\ guarantees\ that\ miniz.c\ pulls\ this\ off\ perfectly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ PNG\ writing:\ See\ the\ tdefl\_write\_image\_to\_png\_file\_in\_memory()\ function,\ originally\ written\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Alex\ Evans.\ Supports\ 1-\/4\ bytes/pixel\ images.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ ZIP\ archive\ API\ notes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ The\ ZIP\ archive\ API's\ where\ designed\ with\ simplicity\ and\ efficiency\ in\ mind,\ with\ just\ enough\ abstraction\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ get\ the\ job\ done\ with\ minimal\ fuss.\ There\ are\ simple\ API's\ to\ retrieve\ file\ information,\ read\ files\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ existing\ archives,\ create\ new\ archives,\ append\ new\ files\ to\ existing\ archives,\ or\ clone\ archive\ data\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ one\ archive\ to\ another.\ It\ supports\ archives\ located\ in\ memory\ or\ the\ heap,\ on\ disk\ (using\ stdio.h),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ or\ you\ can\ specify\ custom\ file\ read/write\ callbacks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Archive\ reading:\ Just\ call\ this\ function\ to\ read\ a\ single\ file\ from\ a\ disk\ archive:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ void\ *mz\_zip\_extract\_archive\_file\_to\_heap(const\ char\ *pZip\_filename,\ const\ char\ *pArchive\_name,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ size\_t\ *pSize,\ mz\_uint\ zip\_flags);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ For\ more\ complex\ cases,\ use\ the\ "{}mz\_zip\_reader"{}\ functions.\ Upon\ opening\ an\ archive,\ the\ entire\ central}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ directory\ is\ located\ and\ read\ as-\/is\ into\ memory,\ and\ subsequent\ file\ access\ only\ occurs\ when\ reading\ individual\ files.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Archives\ file\ scanning:\ The\ simple\ way\ is\ to\ use\ this\ function\ to\ scan\ a\ loaded\ archive\ for\ a\ specific\ file:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ int\ mz\_zip\_reader\_locate\_file(mz\_zip\_archive\ *pZip,\ const\ char\ *pName,\ const\ char\ *pComment,\ mz\_uint\ flags);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ The\ locate\ operation\ can\ optionally\ check\ file\ comments\ too,\ which\ (as\ one\ example)\ can\ be\ used\ to\ identify}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ multiple\ versions\ of\ the\ same\ file\ in\ an\ archive.\ This\ function\ uses\ a\ simple\ linear\ search\ through\ the\ central}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ directory,\ so\ it's\ not\ very\ fast.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Alternately,\ you\ can\ iterate\ through\ all\ the\ files\ in\ an\ archive\ (using\ mz\_zip\_reader\_get\_num\_files())\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ retrieve\ detailed\ info\ on\ each\ file\ by\ calling\ mz\_zip\_reader\_file\_stat().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Archive\ creation:\ Use\ the\ "{}mz\_zip\_writer"{}\ functions.\ The\ ZIP\ writer\ immediately\ writes\ compressed\ file\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ to\ disk\ and\ builds\ an\ exact\ image\ of\ the\ central\ directory\ in\ memory.\ The\ central\ directory\ image\ is\ written}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ all\ at\ once\ at\ the\ end\ of\ the\ archive\ file\ when\ the\ archive\ is\ finalized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ The\ archive\ writer\ can\ optionally\ align\ each\ file's\ local\ header\ and\ file\ data\ to\ any\ power\ of\ 2\ alignment,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ which\ can\ be\ useful\ when\ the\ archive\ will\ be\ read\ from\ optical\ media.\ Also,\ the\ writer\ supports\ placing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ arbitrary\ data\ blobs\ at\ the\ very\ beginning\ of\ ZIP\ archives.\ Archives\ written\ using\ either\ feature\ are\ still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ readable\ by\ any\ ZIP\ tool.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Archive\ appending:\ The\ simple\ way\ to\ add\ a\ single\ file\ to\ an\ archive\ is\ to\ call\ this\ function:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ mz\_bool\ mz\_zip\_add\_mem\_to\_archive\_file\_in\_place(const\ char\ *pZip\_filename,\ const\ char\ *pArchive\_name,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ const\ void\ *pBuf,\ size\_t\ buf\_size,\ const\ void\ *pComment,\ mz\_uint16\ comment\_size,\ mz\_uint\ level\_and\_flags);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ The\ archive\ will\ be\ created\ if\ it\ doesn't\ already\ exist,\ otherwise\ it'll\ be\ appended\ to.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Note\ the\ appending\ is\ done\ in-\/place\ and\ is\ not\ an\ atomic\ operation,\ so\ if\ something\ goes\ wrong}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ during\ the\ operation\ it's\ possible\ the\ archive\ could\ be\ left\ without\ a\ central\ directory\ (although\ the\ local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ file\ headers\ and\ file\ data\ will\ be\ fine,\ so\ the\ archive\ will\ be\ recoverable).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ For\ more\ complex\ archive\ modification\ scenarios:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ 1.\ The\ safest\ way\ is\ to\ use\ a\ mz\_zip\_reader\ to\ read\ the\ existing\ archive,\ cloning\ only\ those\ bits\ you\ want\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ preserve\ into\ a\ new\ archive\ using\ using\ the\ mz\_zip\_writer\_add\_from\_zip\_reader()\ function\ (which\ compiles\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ compressed\ file\ data\ as-\/is).\ When\ you're\ done,\ delete\ the\ old\ archive\ and\ rename\ the\ newly\ written\ archive,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ you're\ done.\ This\ is\ safe\ but\ requires\ a\ bunch\ of\ temporary\ disk\ space\ or\ heap\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ 2.\ Or,\ you\ can\ convert\ an\ mz\_zip\_reader\ in-\/place\ to\ an\ mz\_zip\_writer\ using\ mz\_zip\_writer\_init\_from\_reader(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ append\ new\ files\ as\ needed,\ then\ finalize\ the\ archive\ which\ will\ write\ an\ updated\ central\ directory\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ original\ archive.\ (This\ is\ basically\ what\ mz\_zip\_add\_mem\_to\_archive\_file\_in\_place()\ does.)\ There's\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ possibility\ that\ the\ archive's\ central\ directory\ could\ be\ lost\ with\ this\ method\ if\ anything\ goes\ wrong,\ though.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ ZIP\ archive\ support\ limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ No\ zip64\ or\ spanning\ support.\ Extraction\ functions\ can\ only\ handle\ unencrypted,\ stored\ or\ deflated\ files.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ Requires\ streams\ capable\ of\ seeking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ This\ is\ a\ header\ file\ library,\ like\ stb\_image.c.\ To\ get\ only\ a\ header\ file,\ either\ cut\ and\ paste\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ below\ header,\ or\ create\ miniz.h,\ \#define\ MINIZ\_HEADER\_FILE\_ONLY,\ and\ then\ include\ miniz.c\ from\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ Important:\ For\ best\ perf.\ be\ sure\ to\ customize\ the\ below\ macros\ for\ your\ target\ platform:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \#define\ MINIZ\_USE\_UNALIGNED\_LOADS\_AND\_STORES\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \#define\ MINIZ\_LITTLE\_ENDIAN\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \#define\ MINIZ\_HAS\_64BIT\_REGISTERS\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ On\ platforms\ using\ glibc,\ Be\ sure\ to\ "{}\#define\ \_LARGEFILE64\_SOURCE\ 1"{}\ before\ including\ miniz.c\ to\ ensure\ miniz}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ uses\ the\ 64-\/bit\ variants:\ fopen64(),\ stat64(),\ etc.\ Otherwise\ you\ won't\ be\ able\ to\ process\ large\ files}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ (i.e.\ 32-\/bit\ stat()\ fails\ for\ me\ on\ files\ >\ 0x7FFFFFFF\ bytes).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ MINIZ\_HEADER\_INCLUDED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ MINIZ\_HEADER\_INCLUDED}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00359\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ mz\_deflate()\ compresses\ the\ input\ to\ output,\ consuming\ as\ much\ of\ the\ input\ and\ producing\ as\ much\ output\ as\ possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00360\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00361\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ pStream\ is\ the\ stream\ to\ read\ from\ and\ write\ to.\ You\ must\ initialize/update\ the\ next\_in,\ avail\_in,\ next\_out,\ and\ avail\_out\ members.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00362\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ flush\ may\ be\ MZ\_NO\_FLUSH,\ MZ\_PARTIAL\_FLUSH/MZ\_SYNC\_FLUSH,\ MZ\_FULL\_FLUSH,\ or\ MZ\_FINISH.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00363\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Return\ values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00364\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_OK\ on\ success\ (when\ flushing,\ or\ if\ more\ input\ is\ needed\ but\ not\ available,\ and/or\ there's\ more\ output\ to\ be\ written\ but\ the\ output\ buffer\ is\ full).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00365\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_STREAM\_END\ if\ all\ input\ has\ been\ consumed\ and\ all\ output\ bytes\ have\ been\ written.\ Don't\ call\ mz\_deflate()\ on\ the\ stream\ anymore.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00366\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_STREAM\_ERROR\ if\ the\ stream\ is\ bogus.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00367\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_PARAM\_ERROR\ if\ one\ of\ the\ parameters\ is\ invalid.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00369\ MINIZ\_STATIC\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ mz\_deflate(mz\_streamp\ pStream,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ flush);}

\DoxyCodeLine{00396\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ window\_bits\ must\ be\ MZ\_DEFAULT\_WINDOW\_BITS\ (to\ parse\ zlib\ header/footer)\ or\ -\/MZ\_DEFAULT\_WINDOW\_BITS\ (raw\ deflate).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00398\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00399\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Decompresses\ the\ input\ stream\ to\ the\ output,\ consuming\ only\ as\ much\ of\ the\ input\ as\ needed,\ and\ writing\ as\ much\ to\ the\ output\ as\ possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00400\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00401\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ pStream\ is\ the\ stream\ to\ read\ from\ and\ write\ to.\ You\ must\ initialize/update\ the\ next\_in,\ avail\_in,\ next\_out,\ and\ avail\_out\ members.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00402\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ flush\ may\ be\ MZ\_NO\_FLUSH,\ MZ\_SYNC\_FLUSH,\ or\ MZ\_FINISH.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00403\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ On\ the\ first\ call,\ if\ flush\ is\ MZ\_FINISH\ it's\ assumed\ the\ input\ and\ output\ buffers\ are\ both\ sized\ large\ enough\ to\ decompress\ the\ entire\ stream\ in\ a\ single\ call\ (this\ is\ slightly\ faster).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00404\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_FINISH\ implies\ that\ there\ are\ no\ more\ source\ bytes\ available\ beside\ what's\ already\ in\ the\ input\ buffer,\ and\ that\ the\ output\ buffer\ is\ large\ enough\ to\ hold\ the\ rest\ of\ the\ decompressed\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00405\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Return\ values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00406\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_OK\ on\ success.\ Either\ more\ input\ is\ needed\ but\ not\ available,\ and/or\ there's\ more\ output\ to\ be\ written\ but\ the\ output\ buffer\ is\ full.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00407\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_STREAM\_END\ if\ all\ needed\ input\ has\ been\ consumed\ and\ all\ output\ bytes\ have\ been\ written.\ For\ zlib\ streams,\ the\ adler-\/32\ of\ the\ decompressed\ data\ has\ also\ been\ verified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00408\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_STREAM\_ERROR\ if\ the\ stream\ is\ bogus.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00409\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_DATA\_ERROR\ if\ the\ deflate\ stream\ is\ invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00410\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_PARAM\_ERROR\ if\ one\ of\ the\ parameters\ is\ invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00411\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ MZ\_BUF\_ERROR\ if\ no\ forward\ progress\ is\ possible\ because\ the\ input\ buffer\ is\ empty\ but\ the\ inflater\ needs\ more\ input\ to\ continue,\ or\ if\ the\ output\ buffer\ is\ not\ large\ enough.\ Call\ mz\_inflate()\ again}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00412\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ with\ more\ input\ data,\ or\ with\ more\ room\ in\ the\ output\ buffer\ (except\ when\ using\ single\ call\ decompression,\ described\ above).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00413\ MINIZ\_STATIC\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ mz\_inflate(mz\_streamp\ pStream,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ flush);}

\DoxyCodeLine{00725\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Decompression\ flags\ used\ by\ tinfl\_decompress().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00726\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TINFL\_FLAG\_PARSE\_ZLIB\_HEADER:\ If\ set,\ the\ input\ has\ a\ valid\ zlib\ header\ and\ ends\ with\ an\ adler32\ checksum\ (it's\ a\ valid\ zlib\ stream).\ Otherwise,\ the\ input\ is\ a\ raw\ deflate\ stream.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00727\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TINFL\_FLAG\_HAS\_MORE\_INPUT:\ If\ set,\ there\ are\ more\ input\ bytes\ available\ beyond\ the\ end\ of\ the\ supplied\ input\ buffer.\ If\ clear,\ the\ input\ buffer\ contains\ all\ remaining\ input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00728\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TINFL\_FLAG\_USING\_NON\_WRAPPING\_OUTPUT\_BUF:\ If\ set,\ the\ output\ buffer\ is\ large\ enough\ to\ hold\ the\ entire\ decompressed\ stream.\ If\ clear,\ the\ output\ buffer\ is\ at\ least\ the\ size\ of\ the\ dictionary\ (typically\ 32KB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00729\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TINFL\_FLAG\_COMPUTE\_ADLER32:\ Force\ adler-\/32\ checksum\ computation\ of\ the\ decompressed\ bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00730\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00731\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00732\ \ \ TINFL\_FLAG\_PARSE\_ZLIB\_HEADER\ =\ 1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00733\ \ \ TINFL\_FLAG\_HAS\_MORE\_INPUT\ =\ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00734\ \ \ TINFL\_FLAG\_USING\_NON\_WRAPPING\_OUTPUT\_BUF\ =\ 4,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00735\ \ \ TINFL\_FLAG\_COMPUTE\_ADLER32\ =\ 8}
\DoxyCodeLine{00736\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00737\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00740\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ On\ entry:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00741\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ pSrc\_buf,\ src\_buf\_len:\ Pointer\ and\ size\ of\ the\ Deflate\ or\ zlib\ source\ data\ to\ decompress.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00742\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ On\ return:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00744\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ *pOut\_len\ will\ be\ set\ to\ the\ decompressed\ data's\ size,\ which\ could\ be\ larger\ than\ src\_buf\_len\ on\ uncompressible\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00745\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ The\ caller\ must\ call\ mz\_free()\ on\ the\ returned\ block\ when\ it's\ no\ longer\ needed.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00747\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00823\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ tdefl\_init()\ compression\ flags\ logically\ OR'd\ together\ (low\ 12\ bits\ contain\ the\ max.\ number\ of\ probes\ per\ dictionary\ search):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00824\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_DEFAULT\_MAX\_PROBES:\ The\ compressor\ defaults\ to\ 128\ dictionary\ probes\ per\ dictionary\ search.\ 0=Huffman\ only,\ 1=Huffman+LZ\ (fastest/crap\ compression),\ 4095=Huffman+LZ\ (slowest/best\ compression).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00825\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00826\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00827\ \ \ TDEFL\_HUFFMAN\_ONLY\ =\ 0,\ TDEFL\_DEFAULT\_MAX\_PROBES\ =\ 128,\ TDEFL\_MAX\_PROBES\_MASK\ =\ 0xFFF}
\DoxyCodeLine{00828\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00829\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00830\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_WRITE\_ZLIB\_HEADER:\ If\ set,\ the\ compressor\ outputs\ a\ zlib\ header\ before\ the\ deflate\ data,\ and\ the\ Adler-\/32\ of\ the\ source\ data\ at\ the\ end.\ Otherwise,\ you'll\ get\ raw\ deflate\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00831\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_COMPUTE\_ADLER32:\ Always\ compute\ the\ adler-\/32\ of\ the\ input\ data\ (even\ when\ not\ writing\ zlib\ headers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00832\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_GREEDY\_PARSING\_FLAG:\ Set\ to\ use\ faster\ greedy\ parsing,\ instead\ of\ more\ efficient\ lazy\ parsing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00833\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_NONDETERMINISTIC\_PARSING\_FLAG:\ Enable\ to\ decrease\ the\ compressor's\ initialization\ time\ to\ the\ minimum,\ but\ the\ output\ may\ vary\ from\ run\ to\ run\ given\ the\ same\ input\ (depending\ on\ the\ contents\ of\ memory).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00834\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_RLE\_MATCHES:\ Only\ look\ for\ RLE\ matches\ (matches\ with\ a\ distance\ of\ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00835\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_FILTER\_MATCHES:\ Discards\ matches\ <=\ 5\ chars\ if\ enabled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00836\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_FORCE\_ALL\_STATIC\_BLOCKS:\ Disable\ usage\ of\ optimized\ Huffman\ tables.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00837\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ TDEFL\_FORCE\_ALL\_RAW\_BLOCKS:\ Only\ use\ raw\ (uncompressed)\ deflate\ blocks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00838\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ low\ 12\ bits\ are\ reserved\ to\ control\ the\ max\ \#\ of\ hash\ probes\ per\ dictionary\ lookup\ (see\ TDEFL\_MAX\_PROBES\_MASK).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00839\ \textcolor{keyword}{enum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00840\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00841\ \ \ TDEFL\_WRITE\_ZLIB\_HEADER\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 0x01000,}
